posted:Posted April 1, 2024
msg:After traveling so many times, this hotel stay experience can be said to be a very strange one. Let me talk about the good things first:
1. The hotel is in a prime location and convenient transportation. If you come from Xianyang Airport, you can take the subway with confidence. It is the starting station throughout the journey, so there must be seats. Finally, you can get to the hotel from Exit A of Hepingmen Station, and you don‚Äôt have to walk any extra distance
2. The hotel room is very large (for this price), the bathroom is separated into dry and wet areas, there is an independent cloakroom with a full-body dressing mirror, and two tables are convenient for makeup, which is more friendly to girls
The following is a very embarrassing place:
1. The hotel‚Äôs air conditioner can only blow hot air before summer! Most of the rooms‚Äô fresh air systems also have problems, so even natural wind can‚Äôt blow! We booked two rooms and checked in at the end of March, one at 33-35 degrees and the other at 29 degrees. I suspect that the previous guest didn‚Äôt know that the air conditioner could only blow hot air and kept turning on the cooling for the 35-degree room, which turned into a sauna room. 29 degrees is the normal temperature for a room facing this direction (still hard to fall asleep). The hotel suggested that we sleep with the window open, but all the rooms in this twin room type face the family compound and there is no wind at all. The windows are very small and can only be opened a little bit in the corner. There is also a screen in front, so opening the window has basically no effect except bringing more noise (some people do morning exercises nearby, and it is very loud when they start to crack whips at 5 am). By the way, the hotel does not provide fans. No wonder we saw many room doors open when we checked in. I was wondering what everyone‚Äôs habit was at the time, but later I realized it was too hotü•µ
2. There is no phone in the hotel room! This is the first time I have seen a hotel without a phone. Although there is an LCD screen in front of the bed to call the front desk, it is basically difficult for the front desk to hear you, so you have to use your mobile phone to contact them. Calling itself is fine, but the problem is that if you order takeout, it will be very troublesome. Because there is no phone in the room, the robot cannot notify you when it is delivered, so the takeaway person needs to enter your mobile phone number when delivering the food, but the mobile phone numbers of the takeaway platform are virtual, and they have to call you to confirm, and their operation does not seem to be simple. Anyway, every time I order takeout, the delivery guy can‚Äôt do it himself, and I have to ask the front desk for help again.
3. Communication at the front desk was difficult. There was a little boy who started working without any training. His attitude was good, but the problem was that he couldn't understand what you were saying. It seemed that he couldn't understand your request or the help you needed from him. The check-in time of the hotel was 14:00 in the afternoon, but we couldn't check in at 14:00. His explanation was that there was only one aunt cleaning the first floor and she couldn't clean it up (it was also quite funny. What does it have to do with me?). I said that we should first clean up one room for us, and we can put our luggage there first, and then clean up the other room slowly and give us the room card when we come back in the evening. This logic is not difficult to understand, right? He didn't understand it. Finally, the hotel's attitude to solve the problem was good. When there was a vacancy the next day, we were moved to a room facing the city wall, which was much cooler. It is recommended that everyone try to book this direction if you book a room during March-May, otherwise the temperature of the other direction will be uninhabitable if the problem of their air conditioning system is not solved. Also, I would like to thank the Ctrip platform for helping me communicate. In the end, the hotel refunded us the room fee for the first day when it was very hot.
